sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">其实在发布 Galaxy Note20 和 Galaxy Z Fold 2 之前，三星已经提前把 5G 版的 Galaxy Z Flip 上架，尽管相比年初以「三星第一款竖折手机」的身份登场时要低调许多，但有着「5G」和「骁龙 865 Plus」这两个升级光环，5G 的 Galaxy Z Flip 也还是能吸引到不少人关注。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357784 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC09257-1024x683.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"720\" height=\"480\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC09257-1024x683.jpg 720w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC09257-1024x683-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ <a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/1315241\">Galaxy Z Flip（4G）评测</a></p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">前段时间，我短暂体验了 5G 版 Galaxy Z Flip，对我来说，这款手机单从图片上看和 4G 几乎没有区别，这也是我在体验这款手机之前的心理预期。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1358080 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/25ccb03ab5142279d8583c4986100e5.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/25ccb03ab5142279d8583c4986100e5.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/25ccb03ab5142279d8583c4986100e5-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/25ccb03ab5142279d8583c4986100e5-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/25ccb03ab5142279d8583c4986100e5-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">然而事实上新 Z Flip 的升级都是在「看不见，摸得到」的细节当中，这些细节可能不能说服你改变折叠屏手机的影响，但至少能让人看到三星折叠屏手机的确是在一步一个脚印地成长。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1358071 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02576-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02576-1.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02576-1-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02576-1-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02576-1-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">我一向都不算是个喜欢镜面玻璃后盖的人，当然这是我的主观因素大于客观因素，镜面玻璃后盖能营造出通透惊艳的视觉冲击，但作为一个手汗大的糙汉子，镜面玻璃分分钟能成为指纹收集器。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1358088 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/099.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1333\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/099.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/099-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/099-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/099-1024x682.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">所以，我对这次新 Galaxy Z Flip 换用的磨砂玻璃挺有好感，尤其是黑色为主调的冷山灰，感觉要比之前高档不少。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">但我这次体验的，是和冷山灰一起登场的另一种配色，迷雾金。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-1358074 size-large\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/eaebd564cd4fffde26931bdcaaf530b-683x1024.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"683\" height=\"1024\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/eaebd564cd4fffde26931bdcaaf530b-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/eaebd564cd4fffde26931bdcaaf530b-360x540.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/eaebd564cd4fffde26931bdcaaf530b-768x1152.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 683px) 100vw, 683px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">不知为何，最近金色或是与其接近的暖色系配色又在手机圈里流行了起来，像华为 P40 的晨曦金、OPPO Find X2 Pro 的茶橘、vivo X50 Pro+、三星 Galaxy Note20、Galaxy Z Fold 2 这些旗舰都不乏有香槟金或其他金色元素。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357852 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC5272.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"720\" height=\"480\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC5272.jpg 720w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC5272-360x240.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ OPPO Find X2 Pro 茶橘色</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">但严格来说，这次成批发布的 Galaxy Z Flip、Note20、Z Fold 2 的迷雾金都不算是字面意思上的「金色」，它要比金色表现更加深邃，像打了高斯模糊的铜丝，个人认为用「铜色」来形容会更贴合一些。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357853 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Virtual-Unpacked2020-Lead_main1-1-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"720\" height=\"405\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Virtual-Unpacked2020-Lead_main1-1-1.jpg 720w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Virtual-Unpacked2020-Lead_main1-1-1-360x203.jpg 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">另一个在我上手有明显感知变化的是铰链，本质上 5G 版 Galaxy Z Flip 的铰链结构和 4G 版是相同，三星也没有对外宣传过 5G 版铰链有改良，但 5G 版在开合时却比 4G 版要柔了不少。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1358075 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/fbd1134c99a2ea9b8b83b579729ea13.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/fbd1134c99a2ea9b8b83b579729ea13.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/fbd1134c99a2ea9b8b83b579729ea13-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/fbd1134c99a2ea9b8b83b579729ea13-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/fbd1134c99a2ea9b8b83b579729ea13-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">手机合盖时没有出现很清脆的「啪」一声，而是斯文地「嗒」一声合上，而且合盖时能感觉到铰链阻尼感要比之前更强，合盖动作更加优雅，我想类似的技术也可能会用到 Galaxy Z Fold 2 当中。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1357850 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02579.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"5410\" height=\"3607\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02579.jpg 5410w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02579-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02579-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02579-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 5410px) 100vw, 5410px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ 边角防边框磕碰摩擦的材料是软性橡胶</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">另外根据个人观察，5G 版 Galaxy Z Flip 的金属中框似乎比 4G 版的内卷幅度更大，因而 5G 版内部的黑色塑料边框要比 4G 版更窄，手感要 4G 版要更圆润一些。</span><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">4G 版在展开后边缘手感过渡会有点生硬，但在 5G 版上，手感会自然很多。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357843 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02561.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"5454\" height=\"3636\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02561.jpg 5454w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02561-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02561-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02561-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 5454px) 100vw, 5454px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">屏幕折痕一直是折叠屏手机的老大难问题，即使三星至今已经发布了六款折叠屏手机，也仍然未能根治抢眼的折痕。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">不过折痕在今天似乎不是折叠屏的最大硬伤，毕竟也不会直接影响到正常使用，「是否耐用」、「用着会不会比普通屏幕差」才是大家最关心的地方。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357851 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02581.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02581.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02581-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02581-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02581-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ 亮屏状态下折痕几乎可以被忽略</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">5G 版 Galaxy Z Flip 屏幕表层依然是 UTG 玻璃，但与其说是玻璃，不如说是一层软性贴膜。然而虽说贴膜本身是为了给折叠屏防刮，但贴膜本身的强度并不高，我在正常情况下用了 3 天，贴膜也已经有细微的刮痕。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1358083 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4cfae2d27f19e92f92fafe5d6d2312a.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4cfae2d27f19e92f92fafe5d6d2312a.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4cfae2d27f19e92f92fafe5d6d2312a-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4cfae2d27f19e92f92fafe5d6d2312a-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4cfae2d27f19e92f92fafe5d6d2312a-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">软性贴膜面对手指、空气中的沙粒灰尘摩擦，有刮痕也是无可避免的事情，我们也不能在折叠屏这种柔性面板上要求高强度的防刮材质。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">毕竟高强度意味着更坚硬的材质，而坚硬和折叠屏的柔性违背，所以个人认为在柔性贴膜有刮痕在目前来说是正常情况。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">但我想三星也不妨可以考虑类似于可更换贴膜的方案，毕竟刮痕虽不影响使用，但对屏幕的美感也会有一定影响，谁也不希望售价过万元的手机，展开屏幕会有长长短短的刮痕出现。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1358079 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/d29160155dc2fd03d7e0ae2a9895d54.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/d29160155dc2fd03d7e0ae2a9895d54.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/d29160155dc2fd03d7e0ae2a9895d54-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/d29160155dc2fd03d7e0ae2a9895d54-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/d29160155dc2fd03d7e0ae2a9895d54-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">和外观一样升级明显的是内部的骁龙 865 Plus。其实在刚知道新 Z Flip 用上骁龙 865 Plus 的时候我是挺讶异，因为骁龙 865 Plus 当时还只是在 <a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/1353565\">华硕 ROG</a>、<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/1314068\">黑鲨</a>、<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/1353362\">联想拯救者</a>这几款新游戏手机出现，而这些都是强调性能的肌肉手机，用最新最强的 SoC 也是情理之中，但 Z Flip 显然不是和游戏手机同级的产品，所以之前我也只是预想着新 Z Flip 最多也只会用目前产能更高的骁龙 865，而不是骁龙 865 Plus。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">新 Z Flip 能用上 865 Plus，我想应该也跟三星和高通本身有着较好的代工合作背景有关，在这个背景下，三星也能在下半年的新品中，拔得 Android 阵营骁龙 865 Plus 旗舰的头筹。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">骁龙 865 Plus 可以说是一个让人再次关注新 Z Flip 的升级点，但它对手机日常体验没有太明显的实质变化，除了因为之前骁龙 855 Plus 这个底子本身不差以外，能让 Z Flip 用到高频性能的地方也不算多，所以不论是 855 Plus 还是 865 Plus，在同一套系统下，他们之间的流畅度、反应都几乎一致。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1358091 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/QQ20191114-0-1024x661.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1024\" height=\"661\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/QQ20191114-0-1024x661.jpg 1024w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/QQ20191114-0-1024x661-360x232.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/QQ20191114-0-1024x661-768x496.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ 摩托罗拉 Razr</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">相比于 SoC 在性能上的提升，新 Galaxy Z Flip 升级的核心意义主要还是对 5G 的支持，我甚至曾经认为三星是「升 5G 顺便升 SoC」。这个观点的原因在于 Z Flip 并不是唯一一款竖折屏手机，其他还有<a href=\"https://www.cnbeta.com/articles/tech/998689.htm\">摩托罗拉的新 Razr 也对 5G 跃跃欲试</a>，在 Z Flip 用上 5G，除了能再次提升折叠屏手机的热度，也能帮助三星巩固竖折手机方面的地位，不被其他厂商超越。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">因此，三星为 Galaxy Z Flip 用上 5G 网络配置，个人认为除了有产品因素，也有一定的市场因素所在。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">然而尽管手机用上了骁龙 865 Plus，网络支持也达到了 5G 频段，但手机的内存和存储空间、电池容量相比 4G 版都没有变化，依然还是 8GB 和 256GB 的标准配置，电池容量 3300mAh。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1358090 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5OuKXWawdMy1tfpw.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"800\" height=\"600\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5OuKXWawdMy1tfpw.jpg 800w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5OuKXWawdMy1tfpw-360x270.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5OuKXWawdMy1tfpw-768x576.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 800px) 100vw, 800px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ Galaxy Z Flip（4G）拆解. 图片来自：<a href=\"https://zh.ifixit.com/Guide/%E4%B8%89%E6%98%9F+Galaxy+Z+Flip+%E6%8B%86%E8%A7%A3/131002\">iFixit</a></p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">配置不变的原因估计和 Z Flip 已经寸土寸金的内部空间有关，而作为小改款，5G 版也没必要为了容纳更高的配置从新开模设计机身，因而这次 5G 版也只是对关键的 SoC 进行升级，其余和 4G 版保持不变，算是在最小程度影响里做最大程度的升级。 </span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">不过由于这次对 5G 的支持是在不提升电池容量的条件下增加，因而 5G 版 Z Flip 的净待机总时也缩减到 321 小时，比 4G 版的 418 小时要短不少。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1357785 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/power.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"1200\" height=\"972\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/power.jpg 1200w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/power-360x292.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/power-768x622.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/power-1024x829.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ Galaxy Z Flip（4G 版）续航测试成绩</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">而在实际使用中，4G 版在之前的评测中做到了亮屏接近 6 小时的成绩，虽然我来不及测 5G 版的续航，但由于新机其他关键配置和旧机大致相同，所以我以经验推断，5G 版的亮屏时间大约会在 4.5-5 小时之间，大概和开了 120Hz 高刷新率的 Galaxy S20 差不多。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">5G 版 Galaxy Z Flip 在系统方面和 4G 版一致，但由于竖折手机已经问世有半年之久，现在的 One UI 也已经逐步针对该形态增加了一些能体现出折叠屏优势，或者是能更利用好折叠屏这一特性的「甜点级」功能。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1358077 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/157837998cf54d0395671ccdc1227eb.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"5891\" height=\"3927\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/157837998cf54d0395671ccdc1227eb.jpg 5891w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/157837998cf54d0395671ccdc1227eb-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/157837998cf54d0395671ccdc1227eb-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/157837998cf54d0395671ccdc1227eb-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 5891px) 100vw, 5891px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">比方说相机这方面。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">在之前的 Galaxy Z Flip 中，用户能通过折叠手机的方式把手机变成三脚架，随后通过手势控制相机拍照。而现在，双击相机取景框能把取景框变成半屏，并在上下两部分屏幕中切换显示。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-1357840 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/ec9b84fc-f4e8-4e02-adc1-635442e65732.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"492\" height=\"492\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">这个功能的作用有点像相机里的翻折屏，在把取景框放到下半部分后，我能在较低角度轻松拍下眼前画面，而不用弯下身体观看手机屏幕，或者盲拍。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357844 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02563.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"5985\" height=\"3990\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02563.jpg 5985w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02563-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02563-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02563-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 5985px) 100vw, 5985px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ 别人看我是这样子的</p>\n</div>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357845 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02565.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02565.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02565-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02565-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02565-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ 我看自己是这样的</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">而体现这一功能最有用的地方是在配合超广角相机仰拍的时候，作为拍摄者，我可以不用半蹲在地上拍照，甚至还可以通过超广角和折叠屏创造更多拍摄角度。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357846 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02569.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02569.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02569-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02569-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02569-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">值得一提的是，三星在之前的宣发中不止一次提到 Galaxy Z Flip 折叠自拍的便利优势，而在这次体验期间我无意打开了 B612 这个美颜相机 app，发现 app 已经对折叠屏拍照进行适配，如今第三方软件也能调用原生相机才有的「折屏取景框自动上移」特性，在第三方软件也能用上 Z Flip 的化妆盒形态来自拍。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1357839 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9d657044-33ee-4a35-a613-828e4b2b2e61.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"533\" height=\"533\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9d657044-33ee-4a35-a613-828e4b2b2e61.gif 533w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9d657044-33ee-4a35-a613-828e4b2b2e61-360x360.gif 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 533px) 100vw, 533px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ 软件：B612</p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">智能手机无论是配置还是形态上都有着翻天覆地的变化，不但屏幕边框越做越窄、相机镜头越来越多、拍照像素破亿，手机也从直板变成「化妆盒」。然而即使大家都知道参数变得越来越大，但实际并不理解这些变化会给日常体验带来什么影响，即使是折叠屏，大部分人也只知道它可折叠，却不了解折叠对日常体验的影响和意义。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1358069 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02571-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"6240\" height=\"4160\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02571-1.jpg 6240w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02571-1-360x240.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02571-1-768x512.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02571-1-1024x683.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 6240px) 100vw, 6240px\" /></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">因此，通过用户常用软件或功能去带动用户了解硬件好处，就成了当下手机厂商引导用户接触新技术的方式，比如像这次 Z Flip 的取景框切换、对第三方自拍 app 的支持，就是引导用户知道折叠屏好处的一个入口，改变普通人对折叠屏手机的印象。</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"size-full wp-image-1357782 aligncenter\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/21-1024x520.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"720\" height=\"366\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/21-1024x520.png 720w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/21-1024x520-360x183.png 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p>\n<div class=\"editor-image-source\">\n<p>▲ 三星 Galaxy Z Flip 的 <span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">Thom Browne 定制版</span></p>\n</div>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">三星给 5G 版 Galaxy Z Flip 的定价是 12499 元，整体比 4G 版的 11999 元确实贵了，但从处理器、网络支持、机身这些变化看，500 元差价换来的升级还是比较值得，况且这些都是一劳永逸的升级，更好的配置固然对长时间使用更加有利。</span></p>\n<p class=\"ql-long-7929149\"><span class=\"ql-author-7929149 ql-size-10\">当然，5G 版的角色本质上是 Z Flip 产品的一个补充，而不是取代。为了保持 4G 和 5G 的同步销售，三星依然将潘多拉紫、Thom Browne 定制版作为 4G 版的独有配色。</span></p>\n<p>#欢迎关注爱范儿官方微信公众号：爱范儿（微信号：ifanr），更多精彩内容第一时间为您奉上。</p><p>\n<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com\">爱范儿</a> |\n<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/1357779\">原文链接</a> ·\n<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com/1357779#comments\">查看评论</a> ·\n<a href=\"https://weibo.com/ifanr\">新浪微博</a>\n</p>\n\n<br>\n<div 579.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn55@2020_3/2020/08/16/09-52-59-597_1d2d56c7499a4004.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02561.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn8@2020_6/2020/08/16/09-52-56-985_55f29bef60657e66.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02581.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn35@2020_5/2020/08/16/09-52-44-244_46b70344eb46bd47.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4cfae2d27f19e92f92fafe5d6d2312a.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn31@2020_1/2020/08/16/09-52-57-499_2b864d2c14b29829.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/d29160155dc2fd03d7e0ae2a9895d54.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn47@2020_3/2020/08/16/09-52-53-627_e5154867e2acb69f.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/QQ20191114-0-1024x661.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn95@2020_4/2020/08/16/09-52-58-887_43e8fa960c2b3678.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5OuKXWawdMy1tfpw.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn32@2020_2/2020/08/16/09-52-47-039_118822490abc8a77.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/power.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn92@2020_5/2020/08/16/09-52-52-592_1fc78bfbef226075.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/157837998cf54d0395671ccdc1227eb.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn39@2020_6/2020/08/16/09-52-55-644_a324f22579fb59bf.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/ec9b84fc-f4e8-4e02-adc1-635442e65732.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn31@2020_5/2020/08/16/09-52-41-380_552c5669beec3b8b.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02563.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn40@2020_6/2020/08/16/09-52-59-053_1860cb34ee58a8f5.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn63@2020_2/2020/08/16/09-52-39-930_3f7d4387a94a186b.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02569.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn16@2020_5/2020/08/16/09-52-54-392_635ca6e4ff66201c.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9d657044-33ee-4a35-a613-828e4b2b2e61.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn88@2020_1/2020/08/16/09-52-40-896_174b87a3618cd230.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/DSC02571-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn35@2020_1/2020/08/16/09-52-40-413_d2a00339c55c7b42.webp","https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/21-1024x520.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn31@2020_2/2020/08/16/09-52-43-372_cf2d06bce54f30b3.webp"}},{"createdTime":"2020-08-16 17:52:38","updatedTime":"2020-08-16 17:52:38","title":"对于这样一款透明电视，喊出 Amazing 就够了","link":"https://www.ifanr.com/?p=1358531&utm_source=rss&utm_medium=rss&utm_campaign=","description":"<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358543\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG277.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG277.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG277-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG277-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG277-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>三天前，小米科技的 CEO 雷军通过一场公开演讲总结了小米十年来的历程，小米十年一路走来，免不了一些激动与煽情，一时间现场仿佛艺术人生。</p>\n<p>当演讲来到下半场，熟悉的发布会终于回来了，小米 10 至尊纪念版，Redmi K30 至尊纪念版，以及小米大师 OLED 透明电视，雷军用三款「超大杯」产品一下子将气氛带到了最高潮。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1357936\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/xiaomitoumingdianshi.jpeg\" alt=\"\" width=\"4000\" height=\"2250\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/xiaomitoumingdianshi.jpeg 4000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/xiaomitoumingdianshi-360x203.jpeg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/xiaomitoumingdianshi-768x432.jpeg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/xiaomitoumingdianshi-1024x576.jpeg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 4000px) 100vw, 4000px\" /></p>\n<p>如果说小米 10 至尊纪念版和 Redmi K30 至尊纪念版因为在微博预热已久，热度尚属意料之中，那透明电视则是给了几乎所有人一个大大的惊喜。</p>\n<p>小米这个肌肉秀到位了。</p>\n<p>在把热度让给两位历史更悠久的手机前辈后，今天是小米透明电视「独享的 Moment」。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358542\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG280.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG280.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG280-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG280-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG280-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<h3>三天后我们再看小米透明电视</h3>\n<p>在人多嘈杂的现场之后，今天我们第一次有机会好好的看看第二款小米电视大师系列产品，小米透明电视的所有细节。</p>\n<p>透明，是这款电视第一眼带来的震撼，这种震撼不亚于小米 2016 年第一次发布 MIX 一代时的全面屏设计。当雷军在发布会现场将手放在电视背后，所有人看着那只由像素组成的蝴蝶仿佛真的落在雷军手上时，全场想起了连绵不绝的惊呼。</p>\n<p>而当震撼和兴奋褪去后，再次见到这款透明电视时，如今抱着的更多的是一种欣赏态度。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358546\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG275.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG275.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG275-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG275-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG275-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>但可以肯定的是，所有从实用性角度出发去看待这款电视的都错了，因为这样一款产品只需要酷，只需要让你喊出 Amazing 就可以了。</p>\n<p>首先我们先一起看一下这款小米透明电视的主要规格：</p>\n<p>这块面板无疑来自 LGD，这个透明面板是 LGD 在去年开始量产的产品。尺寸为对角线 55 英寸，比大师系列第一台小了 10 英寸。分辨率为 1920&#215;1080，并非现在流行的 4K 级别。支持 120Hz 刷新率，P3 色域表现达到 93%，支持 10bit 色彩显示，以及透明度达到了 40%。</p>\n<p>从规格上说，这块透明 OLED 面板的数据肯定是要比市面上的非透明 OLED 面板逊色，但毕竟规格并非是这款电视的重点。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358551\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG271.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1125\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG271.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG271-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG271-768x432.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG271-1024x576.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>在电视息屏或者关闭的时候，电视的面板会呈现一种像是叠加了黑色半透明的玻璃，有点像我们上了涂层的车窗玻璃，但没有车窗的颜色那么深，完全能够直接透过看到电视背面的物体。</p>\n<p>也是因为这个半透明的特性，环境光线的强弱对电视显示效果造成的影响会远远超过普通电视。</p>\n<p>在没有外部光源的情况下，小米透明电视的观看效果和普通的电视几无区别，色彩和亮度已经实际的效果都是可以接受的。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358549\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG270.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG270.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG270-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG270-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG270-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>但是在有外部光源的情况下， 比如头顶天花板的大灯，这时候由于有更多的光线穿越过电视，减弱了电视本身发出的光线进入人眼，实际上我们看到的情况就是电视的透明程度越来越高。</p>\n<p>如果把这台电视搬到正午的室外，那么很可能我们将看不见屏幕上任何内容，而只能看到一块半透明的玻璃。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358550\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG276.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG276.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG276-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG276-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG276-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>那如果从电视的背面看过去呢？你会发现几乎看不到画面的内容是什么，看到的只是半透明的对面以及更强烈的屏幕反光。说明 OLED 像素的光线绝大多数都从正面进入了人眼，只朝背后泄露了那么一小部分。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358545\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG274.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1128\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG274.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG274-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG274-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG274-1024x578.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>由于在亮度方面没有并没有找到官方资料，所以无从得知这块屏幕的平均亮度和最大亮度数据，以肉眼的实际观感来看，在黑暗环境下整体的亮度是还是挺好的（图片纹路为相机因素）。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358547\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG272.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1128\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG272.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG272-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG272-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG272-1024x578.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>为了进一步体现它这个透明的效果，小米还把 MIUI For TV 进行了一番定制，在系统的 UI 元素中原先蓝色的地方都替换成了半透明的黑色，和我们常见的普通 MIUI For TV 形成了较大区别。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358555\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG285.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1100\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG285.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG285-360x198.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG285-768x422.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG285-1024x563.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>炫酷够了，但也有一些副作用。前面说了这块面板的透明度表现和环境亮度呈正相关。实际上现场的环境光线的确复杂，尤其是其中一台透明电视的后面直接是生态链产品，白色为主的产品在透明面板下非常扎眼。</p>\n<p>如果环境光线太亮的话，人眼视觉注意力还是很容易就会被后面的白色夺走，而当背景越接近黑色时，显示效果才越接近普通的电视，所以最好关灯使用才能达到最好的视觉效果。</p>\n<h3>一块玻璃板嵌在圆盘上</h3>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358552\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG282.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG282.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG282-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG282-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG282-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>电视本身的设计也值得说道一番。从整个电视的设计来看，非常像一块玻璃板嵌在一个圆形的「底盘」上，单从美学设计上看相当出众的。有人说把主机换成矩形会更好，这点我倒是不同意，因为屏幕面板本身就是矩形，加上透明的特性，其实能够直接看到「底盘」是一个完整的圆形，从而形成了一种几何上的冲突美感。</p>\n<p>而如果是普通的 OLED 面板是看不到位于机身后面的部分，所以也算是小米透明电视一种得天独厚的特性了。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358553\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/P1311133.2020-08-14-06_40_24.gif\" alt=\"\" width=\"720\" height=\"405\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/P1311133.2020-08-14-06_40_24.gif 720w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/P1311133.2020-08-14-06_40_24-360x203.gif 360w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px\" /></p>\n<p>而形成玻璃板视觉的原因在于，这台电视采用了小米擅长的全面屏设计，同时由于不需要背光模组，让侧面看起来非常薄，甚至不足 1cm（官方数据为 5.7mm）。基本上就是两层玻璃盖板夹着 OLED 层。不过面向观众的正面会有一圈金属边框包边。</p>\n<p>电视的电路、芯片和音箱等配置都集成在了这块圆柱体的主机上，小米透明电视内置了 MTK9650 芯片，和 65 英寸的小米电视大师 OLED 的芯片相同，存储也是 3GB+32GB。所以也支持 AI 画质，以及像动态对比度，MEMC 动态补偿等一系列丰富的画质调节选项。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358554\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG284.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG284.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG284-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG284-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG284-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>机身的接口在圆盘底座的后面，具备 3 个 HDMI 2.0 接口，2 个 USB 2.0 接口，1 个 AV 接口，1 个 ATV/DTMB 接口，1 个以太网接口以及 1 个 S/PDIF 光纤接口。</p>\n<p>喇叭方面采用了双通道低音喇叭和一个 20 芯蚕丝高音喇叭协同工作，支持杜比全景声音效，不过整体上感觉效果不如 65 英寸的小米电视大师 OLED。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358541\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG279.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG279.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG279-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG279-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG279-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<h3>够酷就够了</h3>\n<p>相比规格堆到顶的小米 10 至尊纪念版和性价比杀疯了的 K30 至尊纪念版，小米电视这个超大杯的透明电视给人的感觉更多还是概念产品。</p>\n<p>如今小米宣布他们已经有能力量产这款电视，这让愿意以 49999 元的尝鲜的用户，能够真正把这台透明电视抱回家看。透明到底有什么好呢？它代表的更多是科技领域的一次尝试和对未来的探索。</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-1358548\" src=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG278.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1127\" srcset=\"https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG278.jpg 2000w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG278-360x203.jpg 360w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG278-768x433.jpg 768w, https://s3.ifanr.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/WechatIMG278-1024x577.jpg 1024w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 2000px) 100vw, 2000px\" /></p>\n<p>你越是围绕这款透明电视去仔细打量，这种感觉就越明显，越是觉得这款产品和普通的电视并不是一回事，也不应该被拿来进行比较。它不该出现在普通的家居环境中，而似乎应该是一个陈列品，一个高级的摆设。</p>\n<p>也只有用这样的角度去审视它，你才会感觉到它的价值和美在哪里。如果你一开始就奔着实用性去，那我想你从根本上就来错了地方。</p>\n<p>随着科技的发展，以后人人都会看上透明的电视吗，极大概率是不会的，沉浸式的 VR 明显是一种更出色的方案，而透明屏幕的实用性则堪忧。</p>\n<p>那为什么我们依旧觉得一款透明电视很酷？因为它颠覆了我们对常规电视的认知，能让你喊出 Amazing 不是就够了吗？</p>\n<p>#欢迎关注爱范儿官方微信公众号：爱范儿（微信号：ifanr），更多精彩内容第一时间为您奉上。</p><p>\n<a href=\"https://www.ifanr.com\">爱范儿</a>
